###  Länsiauto₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Länsiauto* (westcar)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  1
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  ORG
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
